## 18 Introduction to Paging

首先了解一下程序的参数和默认值

```python
parser = OptionParser()
# 虚拟地址，用逗号分隔
parser.add_option('-A', '--addresses', default='-1',
                  help='a set of comma-separated pages to access; -1 means randomly generate', 
                  action='store', type='string', dest='addresses')
# 随机种子
parser.add_option('-s', '--seed',    default=0,     help='the random seed',                               action='store', type='int', dest='seed')
# 地址空间大小，默认为 16k
parser.add_option('-a', '--asize',   default='16k', help='address space size (e.g., 16, 64k, 32m, 1g)',   action='store', type='string', dest='asize')
# 物理内存大小，默认为 64k
parser.add_option('-p', '--physmem', default='64k', help='physical memory size (e.g., 16, 64k, 32m, 1g)', action='store', type='string', dest='psize')
# 页大小，默认为 4k
parser.add_option('-P', '--pagesize', default='4k', help='page size (e.g., 4k, 8k, whatever)',            action='store', type='string', dest='pagesize')
# 随机生成的虚拟地址数量，默认为 5
parser.add_option('-n', '--numaddrs',  default=5,  help='number of virtual addresses to generate',       action='store', type='int', dest='num')
# 虚拟地址空间到物理空间的映射有效，默认为 50%，即 1/2 的页无效
parser.add_option('-u', '--used',       default=50, help='percent of virtual address space that is used', action='store', type='int', dest='used')
# 详细模式
parser.add_option('-v',                             help='verbose mode',                                  action='store_true', default=False, dest='verbose')
# 计算答案
parser.add_option('-c',                             help='compute answers for me',                        action='store_true', default=False, dest='solve')

(options, args) = parser.parse_args()
```

线性页表（linear page table）
- 页表格条目（page table entry, PTE）
  - 有效位（valid bit）
  - 物理帧号（physical frame number, PFN）
      - 物理页号（physical page number, PPN） 

虚拟地址
- 虚拟页面号（virtual page number, VPN）
- 页内偏移量（offset）

使用默认参数运行
- 地址空间 16k，页大小 4k
  - 4 张页表，2 位区分页表，12 位偏移量
  - 利用十六进制的倒数第四位区分页表
- 页表有效位（最左边的最高位）
  - 1 有效
  - 0 无效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0                  <---- 随机种子
ARG address space size 16k  <---- 地址空间大小
ARG phys mem size 64k       <---- 物理内存大小
ARG page size 4k            <---- 页大小
ARG verbose True            <---- 详细输出
ARG addresses -1            <---- 随机生成虚拟地址列表


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x8000000c        <---- PFN 0xc
  [       1]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       2]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       3]  0x80000006        <---- PFN 0x6

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x00003229 (decimal:    12841) --> 00006229 (decimal    25129) [VPN 3]     <---- 11 0010 0010 1001 -> 11 = 3, 偏移 0x229
  VA 0x00001369 (decimal:     4969) -->  Invalid (VPN 1 not valid)              <---- 01 0011 0110 1001 -> 01 = 1 
  VA 0x00001e80 (decimal:     7808) -->  Invalid (VPN 1 not valid)              <---- 01 1110 1000 0000 -> 01 = 1 
  VA 0x00002556 (decimal:     9558) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)              <---- 10 0101 0101 0110 -> 10 = 2 
  VA 0x00003a1e (decimal:    14878) --> 00006a1e (decimal    27166) [VPN 3]     <---- 11 1010 0001 1110 -> 11 = 3, 偏移 0xa1e
```

### 1

页大小固定，线性页表的大小随着地址空间的增大而增大
- 地址空间越大，页表越大

<details>
  <summary>地址空间为 1m 的运行结果</summary>

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 1m -p 512m -n 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1m
ARG phys mem size 512m
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
```

<details>
  <summary>地址空间为 2m 的运行结果</summary>

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 2m -p 512m -n 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 2m
ARG phys mem size 512m
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.
```

<details>
  <summary>地址空间为 4m 的运行结果</summary>

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 4m -p 512m -n 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 4m
ARG phys mem size 512m
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.
```

</details>
</br>

地址空间固定，线性页表的大小随着页大小的增大而减小
- 页越大，页表越小

<details>
  <summary>页表大小为 1k 的运行结果</summary>

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 1m -p 512m -n 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1m
ARG phys mem size 512m
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
```

<details>
  <summary>页表大小为 2k 的运行结果</summary>

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 2k -a 1m -p 512m -n 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1m
ARG phys mem size 512m
ARG page size 2k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.
```

### 2

使用 `-u` 参数更改分配给地址空间的页数（百分数）
- 地址空间 16k，页大小 1k，总共有 16 页，使用 4 位区分
  - 4 + 10 = 14 位

1. `-u 0` 页全部无效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 16k -p 32k -u 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0                  <---- 随机种子
ARG address space size 16k  <---- 地址空间大小
ARG phys mem size 32k       <---- 物理内存大小
ARG page size 1k            <---- 页大小
ARG verbose True            <---- 详细输出
ARG addresses -1            <---- 随机生成虚拟地址列表


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x00000000
  [       1]  0x00000000
  [       2]  0x00000000
  [       3]  0x00000000
  [       4]  0x00000000
  [       5]  0x00000000
  [       6]  0x00000000
  [       7]  0x00000000
  [       8]  0x00000000
  [       9]  0x00000000
  [      10]  0x00000000
  [      11]  0x00000000
  [      12]  0x00000000
  [      13]  0x00000000
  [      14]  0x00000000
  [      15]  0x00000000

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x00003a39 (decimal:    14905) -->  Invalid (VPN 14 not valid)     <---- 11 1010 0011 1001 -> 11 10 = 14
  VA 0x00003ee5 (decimal:    16101) -->  Invalid (VPN 15 not valid)     <---- 11 1110 1110 0101 -> 11 11 = 15
  VA 0x000033da (decimal:    13274) -->  Invalid (VPN 12 not valid)     <---- 11 0011 1101 1010 -> 11 00 = 12
  VA 0x000039bd (decimal:    14781) -->  Invalid (VPN 14 not valid)     <---- 11 1001 1011 1101 -> 11 10 = 14
  VA 0x000013d9 (decimal:     5081) -->  Invalid (VPN 4 not valid)      <---- 01 0011 1101 1001 -> 01 00 = 4
```

2. `-u 25` 25% 的页有效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 16k -p 32k -u 25 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 32k
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x80000018        <---- 有效
  [       1]  0x00000000
  [       2]  0x00000000
  [       3]  0x00000000
  [       4]  0x00000000
  [       5]  0x80000009        <---- 有效
  [       6]  0x00000000
  [       7]  0x00000000
  [       8]  0x80000010        <---- 有效
  [       9]  0x00000000
  [      10]  0x80000013        <---- 有效
  [      11]  0x00000000
  [      12]  0x8000001f        <---- 有效
  [      13]  0x8000001c        <---- 有效
  [      14]  0x00000000
  [      15]  0x00000000

  VA 0x00003986 (decimal:    14726) -->  Invalid (VPN 14 not valid)             <---- 11 1001 1000 0110 -> 11 10 = 14
  VA 0x00002bc6 (decimal:    11206) --> 00004fc6 (decimal    20422) [VPN 10]    <---- 10 1011 1100 0110 -> 10 10 = 10
  VA 0x00001e37 (decimal:     7735) -->  Invalid (VPN 7 not valid)              <---- 01 1110 0011 0111 -> 01 11 = 7
  VA 0x00000671 (decimal:     1649) -->  Invalid (VPN 1 not valid)              <---- 00 0110 0111 0001 -> 00 01 = 1
  VA 0x00001bc9 (decimal:     7113) -->  Invalid (VPN 6 not valid)              <---- 01 1011 1100 1001 -> 01 10 = 6
```

3. `-u 50` 50% 的页有效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 16k -p 32k -u 50 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 32k
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x80000018        <---- 有效
  [       1]  0x00000000
  [       2]  0x00000000
  [       3]  0x8000000c        <---- 有效
  [       4]  0x80000009        <---- 有效
  [       5]  0x00000000

  [      12]  0x8000000f        <---- 有效

  [      14]  0x00000000
  [      15]  0x80000008        <---- 有效

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x00003385 (decimal:    13189) --> 00003f85 (decimal    16261) [VPN 12]    <---- 11 0011 1000 0101 -> 11 00 = 12
  VA 0x0000231d (decimal:     8989) -->  Invalid (VPN 8 not valid)              <---- 10 0011 0001 1101 -> 10 00 = 8
  VA 0x000000e6 (decimal:      230) --> 000060e6 (decimal    24806) [VPN 0]     <---- 00 0000 1110 0110 -> 00 00 = 0
  VA 0x00002e0f (decimal:    11791) -->  Invalid (VPN 11 not valid)             <---- 10 1110 0000 1111 -> 10 11 = 11
  VA 0x00001986 (decimal:     6534) --> 00007586 (decimal    30086) [VPN 6]     <---- 01 1001 1000 0110 -> 01 10 = 6
```

4. `-u 75` 75% 的页有效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 16k -p 32k -u 75 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 32k
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x80000018
  [       1]  0x80000008
  [       2]  0x8000000c
  [       3]  0x80000009
  [       4]  0x80000012
  [       5]  0x80000010
  [       6]  0x8000001f
  [       7]  0x8000001c
  [       8]  0x80000017
  [       9]  0x80000015
  [      10]  0x80000003
  [      11]  0x80000013
  [      12]  0x8000001e
  [      13]  0x8000001b
  [      14]  0x80000019
  [      15]  0x80000000

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x00002e0f (decimal:    11791) --> 00004e0f (decimal    19983) [VPN 11]    <---- 10 1110 0000 1111 -> 10 11 = 11
  VA 0x00001986 (decimal:     6534) --> 00007d86 (decimal    32134) [VPN 6]     <---- 01 1001 1000 0110 -> 01 10 = 6
  VA 0x000034ca (decimal:    13514) --> 00006cca (decimal    27850) [VPN 13]    <---- 11 0100 1100 1010 -> 11 01 = 13
  VA 0x00002ac3 (decimal:    10947) --> 00000ec3 (decimal     3779) [VPN 10]    <---- 10 1010 1100 0011 -> 10 10 = 10
  VA 0x00000012 (decimal:       18) --> 00006012 (decimal    24594) [VPN 0]     <---- 00 0000 0001 0010 -> 00 00 = 0
```

5. `-u 100` 页全部有效

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1k -a 16k -p 32k -u 100 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 32k
ARG page size 1k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x80000018
  [       1]  0x80000008
  [       2]  0x8000000c
  [       3]  0x80000009
  [       4]  0x80000012
  [       5]  0x80000010
  [       6]  0x8000001f
  [       7]  0x8000001c
  [       8]  0x80000017
  [       9]  0x80000015
  [      10]  0x80000003
  [      11]  0x80000013
  [      12]  0x8000001e
  [      13]  0x8000001b
  [      14]  0x80000019
  [      15]  0x80000000

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x00002e0f (decimal:    11791) --> 00004e0f (decimal    19983) [VPN 11]    <---- 10 1110 0000 1111 -> 10 11 = 11
  VA 0x00001986 (decimal:     6534) --> 00007d86 (decimal    32134) [VPN 6]     <---- 01 1001 1000 0110 -> 01 10 = 6
  VA 0x000034ca (decimal:    13514) --> 00006cca (decimal    27850) [VPN 13]    <---- 11 0100 1100 1010 -> 11 01 = 13
  VA 0x00002ac3 (decimal:    10947) --> 00000ec3 (decimal     3779) [VPN 10]    <---- 10 1010 1100 0011 -> 10 10 = 10
  VA 0x00000012 (decimal:       18) --> 00006012 (decimal    24594) [VPN 0]     <---- 00 0000 0001 0010 -> 00 00 = 0
```

### 3

物理内存大小为 1024 字节，地址空间大小为 32 字节，页大小为 8 字节，共有 4 页，使用 2 位区分。
- 2 + 3 = 5 位

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 8 -a 32 -p 1024 -s 1 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 1
ARG address space size 32
ARG phys mem size 1024
ARG page size 8
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       1]  0x80000061        <---- 有效
  [       2]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       3]  0x00000000        <---- 无效

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x0000000e (decimal:       14) --> 0000030e (decimal      782) [VPN 1] <---- 0 1110 -> 0 1 = 1
  VA 0x00000014 (decimal:       20) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)          <---- 1 0100 -> 1 0 = 2
  VA 0x00000019 (decimal:       25) -->  Invalid (VPN 3 not valid)          <---- 1 1001 -> 1 1 = 3
  VA 0x00000003 (decimal:        3) -->  Invalid (VPN 0 not valid)          <---- 0 0011 -> 0 0 = 0
  VA 0x00000000 (decimal:        0) -->  Invalid (VPN 0 not valid)          <---- 0 0000 -> 0 0 = 0
```

物理内存大小为 1m，地址空间大小为 32k，页大小为 8k，共有 4 页，使用 2 位区分。
- 2 + 13 = 15 位

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 8k -a 32k -p 1m -s 2 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 2
ARG address space size 32k
ARG phys mem size 1m
ARG page size 8k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1


The format of the page table is simple:
The high-order (left-most) bit is the VALID bit.
  If the bit is 1, the rest of the entry is the PFN.
  If the bit is 0, the page is not valid.
Use verbose mode (-v) if you want to print the VPN # by
each entry of the page table.

Page Table (from entry 0 down to the max size)
  [       0]  0x80000079        <---- 有效
  [       1]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       2]  0x00000000        <---- 无效
  [       3]  0x8000005e        <---- 有效

Virtual Address Trace
  VA 0x000055b9 (decimal:    21945) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)  <---- 101 0101 1011 1001 -> 10 = 2
  VA 0x00002771 (decimal:    10097) -->  Invalid (VPN 1 not valid)  <---- 010 0111 0111 0001 -> 01 = 1
  VA 0x00004d8f (decimal:    19855) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)  <---- 100 1101 1000 1111 -> 10 = 2
  VA 0x00004dab (decimal:    19883) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)  <---- 100 1101 1010 1011 -> 10 = 2
  VA 0x00004a64 (decimal:    19044) -->  Invalid (VPN 2 not valid)  <---- 100 1010 0110 0100 -> 10 = 2
```

物理内存大小为 512m，地址空间大小为 256m，页大小为 1m，共有 256 页，使用 8 位区分。

</br>

### 4

设置参数，让程序无法工作。然后看一看源代码就知道会有哪些原因导致程序退出:)

1. 地址空间大小必须小于物理内存大小

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -a 64k -p 64k -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 64k
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error: physical memory size must be GREATER than address space size (for this simulation)
```

2. 地址空间大小必须是 2 的幂

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -a 1023 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1023
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error in argument: address space must be a multiple of the pagesize
```

3. 页大小必须是 2 的幂

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -P 1023 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 1023
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error in argument: address space must be a multiple of the pagesize
```

4. 地址空间必须大于 1

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -a 1 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error in argument: address space must be a multiple of the pagesize
```

5. 物理内存大小必须大于 0

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -a 0 -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 0
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error: must specify a non-zero address-space size.
```

6. 地址空间必须小于 1g

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -a 1g -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 1g
ARG phys mem size 64k
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error: physical memory size must be GREATER than address space size (for this simulation)
```

7. 物理内存大小必须小于 1g

```bash
./paging-linear-translate.py -p 1g -v -c

# 输出
ARG seed 0
ARG address space size 16k
ARG phys mem size 1g
ARG page size 4k
ARG verbose True
ARG addresses -1

Error: must use smaller sizes (less than 1 GB) for this simulation.
```
